I don't know what it is about Disney XD Sitcoms in the 2010s, but I've always found them to be strangely relaxing to watch, to the point where they've helped me get through having depression. They're all such "turn-your-brain-off" type shows that require no thought or interpretation to be enjoyed. The writing is just good enough to be amusing but mid enough not elicit any stronge emotions, plots are predictable and not gripping enough to be stressful, and they're usually just straight up goofy and (as my mom likes to put it) dorky most of the time. They almost feel like shows that a middle schooler would imagine out of boredom, and it brings me back to simpler times of childhood before the weight of the world started to get so overbearing.

The lanky, nerdy and immature audience self-insert of the main protag of a show that has comedy always has this crush. It's always the smart hot girl who is made flawlessly intelligent and mature and extremely skilled at things to prove shes actually a strong female character, and not just the trophy prize wish-fulfillment hottest girl in school gf  But she is. She always is. You know exactly what her character role is going to be, and what her arc will be and how their relationship will play out  She'll start off annoyed by the main characters goofiness and stupidness, and She'll have been an extremely talented and skilled prodigy who earned her place in whatever thing the main character suddenly forced his way into being at the top of due to his protagonist birthright and plot armour, and She'll resent him for it because he's so dumb, immature and unskilled and he didnt work for the position he got and doesn't deserve it. He will have a crush at first sight on her, and she will hate him intensely at first whenever his protagonist powers give him a one-up over her and he beats her at something she works super hard for and that makes her furious, especially if it's a public defeat where shes humiliated and storms off, then over time she sees his soft heart and the potential within him and starts to warm up, but he's still a manchild and that's all she sees him as until the end of the series and he finally reaches his protag potential   Her flaws are being bossy and a control freak who doesn't know how to let loose, and that's something he has to teach her to do and show her the fun side of life, but mostly she's just annoyed by his antics and would never imagine dating him  You can probably picture countless examples of this character and this dynamic as shes in both movies, games and TV shows
